# Fetch a payment

GET https://api.yoco.com/v1/payments/{payment_id}

Fetch a payment

**Required scope: `business/orders:read`**

Reference: https://yoco.docs.buildwithfern.com/api-reference/yoco-api/payments/fetch-payment-v-1-payments-payment-id-get

## OpenAPI Specification

```yaml
openapi: 3.1.0
info:
  title: yoco-api
  version: 1.0.0
paths:
  /v1/payments/{payment_id}:
    get:
      operationId: fetch-payment-v-1-payments-payment-id-get
      summary: Fetch a payment
      description: |-
        Fetch a payment

        **Required scope: `business/orders:read`**
      tags:
        - subpackage_payments
      parameters:
        - name: payment_id
          in: path
          description: The unique identifier of the payment.
          required: true
          schema:
            type: string
        - name: Authorization
          in: header
          description: JWT authentication
          required: true
          schema:
            type: string
      responses:

              schema:

            For example, when the `currency` is `ZAR`, the `amount` is in cents.
        currency:
          type: string
          description: The currency code in ISO 4217 format.
      required:
        - amount
        - currency
      description: \u003e-
        `Money` represents a monetary value denoted by both an amount and a
        currency.


        The `amount` is always going to be the smallest denomination of the
        given currency. As an example, when dealing

        with South African Rands (ZAR), the amount is in cents.

        eg: R150.45 is therefore represented by `Money(amount=15045,
        currency="ZAR")`.
      title: Money

          type: string
          description: The currency code in ISO 4217 format.
        display_name:
          type: string
          description: A human-friendly label for the refund.
        id:

          description: The unique identifier of the refund.

            - string

          description: The amount of this payment that has been refunded, if any.
        refunds:
          type: array
          items:
            $ref: '#/components/schemas/Refund'
          description: The refunds that have been issued against the payment.
        status:
          $ref: '#/components/schemas/PaymentStatus'

            error.

            - string

      required:

      description: \u003e-
        `ErrorDetail` contains additional error information to accompany an
        `ErrorResponse`.  It is an extension on the

        "problem detail" JSON response modelled in
        https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc9457.html.


        As an example, in the event of a 400 "Validation Error" type response,
        the response may contain one or many

        `ErrorDetail` records with more specific information on each field that
        failed validation.
      title: ErrorDetail
    ErrorResponse:
      type: object
      properties:

          $ref: '#/components/schemas/ErrorCode'

        detail:
          type: string

        errors:
          type:
            - array
            - 'null'

            $ref: '#/components/schemas/ErrorDetail'
          description: \u003e-
            A list of further error details to accompany a problem details
            response.
        status:
          type: integer
          description: A HTTP status code generated by the server.
        title:
          type: string
          description: A short human-readable summary of the problem.
        type:
          type: string
          description: A URI reference that identifies the type of problem.
      required:
        - code
        - detail
        - status
        - title
        - type
      description: |-
        `ErrorResponse` is a RFC 7807 aka "problem details" compatible response.

        See the following references:
        - https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc9457.html
        - https://problems-registry.smartbear.com/
      title: ErrorResponse
  securitySchemes:
    Bearer:
      type: http
      scheme: bearer
      description: JWT authentication
```

## SDK Code Examples

```python
import requests

url = "https://api.yoco.com/v1/payments/payment_id"

headers = {"Authorization": "Bearer \u003ctoken\u003e"}

response = requests.get(url, headers=headers)

print(response.json())
```

```javascript
const url = 'https://api.yoco.com/v1/payments/payment_id';
const options = {method: 'GET', headers: {Authorization: 'Bearer \u003ctoken\u003e'}};

try {
  const response = await fetch(url, options);
  const data = await response.json();
  console.log(data);
} catch (error) {
  console.error(error);
}
```

```go
package main

import (
\t"fmt"
\t"net/http"
```
